The information contained in this directory was compiled by the Personnel Office and the Student Government of the University ofNotre Dame. Student ad­dresses are those that were turned in at registration or corrected at the Student Government Office before October 2, 1966. Persons wishing to make corrections should send their name, address and the correction to either the Student Govern­ment Office or Personnel Office, c/o Student-Staff-Faculty Directory. If suf­
ficient corrections are received, asupplement to this Directory willbe published later this year. 

Operating Instructions for Centrex 
Operating 

FORINFORMATIONOFFCAMPUS-Dial 113. (Do not dial 9.) 
FOR INFORMATION ON CAMPUS -Dial "O' Zero. 
LONG DISTANCE CALLS-OUTGOING -Dial 
9. On second dial tone dial "O". Indiana Belloperator will then place your call. Only outgoing collect or credit card calls will be accepted. 
LONG DISTANCE CALLS-INCOMING -Are notto beacceptedfrom any source. A penalty of $5.00 will be assessed bythe University for eachcollectto11callacceptedby a student. 
CREDIT CARDS-Willnotbe issued on dorm­itory telephones. Student desiringcreditcardsshouldobtainthem throughtheir parents home telephone numbers. 
LOCAL OFF CAMPUS CALLS -Dial 9 then dialthedesiredlocaltelephonenumber. These 
are free calls anywhereinSouthBend, Mish­awaka, Osceola, and Niles, Michigan. Your South Bend Directory lists these numbers. 

REPAIRSERVICE -If yourphone*is not work­ing properly, go to another nearby telephone, dial"O'' for your Notre Dame switchboard op­erator and report it to her. 
ON CAMPUS -Dialthedesiredfour-digitnum­ber as indicated in this directory. 
CONFERENCECALLS can be placed from any station on campus by dialing "5" for the con­ference operator. It is possibleto have 5con­ferees on one conference call. 
TRANSFERRING INCOMING calls to another station on the campus can be accomplished bydepressingtheplungercompletely down. Hold in this position for about 1 second -release and you will receive a ring. Wait for the op-
LOCAL -Dial "9" for outside line, then dial numberaslisted in the SouthBend-Mishawaka directory. 
LONGDISTANCE -Onall long-distance calls, whenthe operator asks for your number, give her 284 and the number assigned to you. Do not give 284-6011. 
Station-to-Station -Dial "9" for outside line, thendial "1" for direct distance dialing equip­mentthen dial the area code and identification number of the distant party. 
Person-to-person -Dial "9" for outside line, then dial "0" for Indiana Bell operator, give her the area code, telephone number and the person you wish to contact.

The public impressions of a university and of you personally are made up of countless things. Few things are more important than your telephone personality. To aid the University's public relations, as well as your own, this directory has been compiled through the efforts of the staff and published by INSTITUTIONAL DIRECTORIES. Every effort has been made to have correct and valid information throughout this directory. Inquiries pertaining to any portion of this publi­cation should be addressed to INSTITUTIONAL DIRECTORIES, Box 283, Lubbock, Texas . . .
